---
title: Glossarium Azteco-Latinum et Latino-Aztecum 
author: Bernardini Biondelli
---

> This is a mirror of a digitatization of an Aztec-Latin dictionary by the Internet Archive. Aztec is also known as Nahuatl, and is one of dozens of native languages spoken in Mexico. The dictionary has some mysterious origins to me, it was published in the mid 1800s but I'm unsure of when the data was gathered and by who. Regardless, I've found it useful for finding a few choice words. I believe the Mexican government and linguists have taken more steps to digitize and proliferate knowledge of the Nahuatl language, but I'm mirroring this old book for history's sake.

- FeLiNa


## Digitized by the Internet Archive in 2010 with funding from University of Toronto 

http://www.archive.org/details/glossariumaztecoOObion
